Grand Prix Oakland Top 9-32 Decklists
=====================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on January 10, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/calderaro.jpg)
By Marc Calderaro











Hey, you guys like decklists? Here are some of those. Sometimes just the Top 8 just isn't enough, right? Well, I've got your fix right here.
